Subject: R&S PCO 81028 - PCI - OT for 1/17/2020 and 1/18/2020 - Carpenter Holidays
PCO Type: **Owner Directed Change**
PCO Category: **Change Condition**
Dear Chris ,
We are pleased to present you with R&S PCO 81028 in the amount of $30,510.00. This work is for PCI - OT for
1/17/2020 and 1/18/2020 - Carpenter Holidays.
The scope of work is as follows:
Cost associated to work PCI OT on 1/17/2020 and 1/18/2020. This OT will help to progress the work as follow:
Work for Friday 1/17/2020
Carpenters = 42
1. Complete framing at Fitness Center Restroom and locker rooms.
2. Rework at EZ Jambs, B4 Close up, Elevator Shafts at Area 1 Level 1
3. Rework at EZ Jambs, B4 Framing, Janitor rooms frame/ hang at Area 1 Level 2
4. Hang Feature wall and ceilings, Base reveal, Skylight framing at Area 2 Level 2
5. C3 Soffit/ Wall hang at Area 3 Level 1
6. C1 Soffit/ Wall hang, C4 Tile backer board/ wall hang at Area 3 Level 2
7. Layout for stone wall coordination and clip install, area 3 exterior
8. Elevator Shafts at roof.
Work for Saturday 1/18/2020
Carpenters = 42
1. Complete framing at Fitness Center Restroom and locker rooms.
2. Rework at EZ Jambs, B4 Close up, Elevator Shafts at Area 1 Level 1
3. Rework at EZ Jambs, B4 Framing, Janitor rooms frame/ hang at Area 1 Level 2
4. Hang Feature wall and ceilings, Base reveal, Skylight framing at Area 2 Level 2
5. C3 Soffit/ Wall hang at Area 3 Level 1
6. C1 Soffit/ Wall hang, C4 Tile backer board/ wall hang at Area 3 Level 2
7. Layout for stone wall coordination and clip install, area 3 exterior
8. Elevator Shafts at roof.
Tapers = 14
1. Outside perimeter 1st coat work at Area 1 Level 2
2. Outside perimeter 1st coat work at Area 2 Level 1
3. C3/C4 first coat at Area 3 Level 1
This OT will help on progressing tile at restrooms, paint and finishes to continue. By working PCI tapers Friday and
Saturday it will help with the time required for the next pass to be applied.
If you have any questions, or if I can be of any further assistance, please feel free to contact me.
Very truly yours,
**Rudolph & Sletten, Inc.**
Edwin Magana
Senior Project Manager

Subject: Microsoft Silicon Valley Campus
PCO #80519 Approval Letter – GMP Deficit Reduction
Dear Kristen,
OAC Services received your revised letter dated March 17 th , 2019 and the changes for PCO 80519 is approved
based on the following conditions –
1. In order to remove the GMP Deficit authorized in CO#3 PSR 3, the project team worked resolve GMP PCO
Allowances to replenish the Rudolph and Sletten, Inc Incentive Fee: Budget (at 0.25%).
2. Adjustments identified in this approved change makes the following Contract Price adjustments:
a. “Cost of Work” value of the “Guaranteed Maximum Price” reduces by $741,618
b. “Incentive Fee Reduction” of the increases by $741,618, thus changes from <$741,618> to $0
c. “Contractor Budget Incentive Fee at 0.25% increased by $741,618, thus changes from $48,085 to $789,703
d. “Microsoft Owners Contingency” does not change.
3. The Net value of PCO 80519 and the impact to the Guaranteed Maximum Price is: < **$741,618>**
a. The table below displays the specific PCO’s that PCO 80519 uses to reduce the GMP PCO Allowances:

Subject: R&S PCO 80576 - GBI - North Sidewalk Out-of-Sequence Work
PCO Category: **Field Condition**
Dear Chris:
We are pleased to present you with R&S PCO 80576 in the amount of $47,834.00. This work is for GBI - North
Sidewalk Out-of-Sequence Work.
The scope of work is as follows:
The entire north side of the project was originally planned to be demoed in one high production activity. At
this point, the scope is chopped out to different activities and per field walk on 06/24/2019, grading a flat area
5 feet from the end of the building and sloping away 10' from the hinge point is required.
This PCO covers GBI original production credit which was to cut adjacent areas to provide fill to grade the
entire north side with a scraper. The new out-of-sequence work requires loading from the south stockpile and
trucking material for soil placement and because of access, the work will be performed with an excavator, pad
drum, skip loader, and added trucking to haul.
If you have any questions, or if I can be of any further assistance, please feel free to contact me.
Yours sincerely,
**Rudolph & Sletten, Inc.**
Chris Moreton
